(**********************************************************************

 The continuation model of the enriched effect calculus

 In this file, we formalize Example 6.10 from the following paper:

   http://www.itu.dk/people/mogel/papers/eec.pdf

 The example considers a specific model of the enriched effect calculus
 such that the monad associated to the adjunction is the continuation
 monad. Most of the building blocks of the model are already present in
 other files, namely limits and colimits in the self-enriched category
 and limits and colimits in the opposite enriched category. The only
 missing part is the construction of the required adjunction.

 Contents:
 1. Continuation adjunction
 1.1. The functors
 1.2. The unit and counit
 1.3. The adjunction
 2. The continuation model

 **********************************************************************)

(**
 1. Continuation adjunction
 *)
Section ContinuationAdjunction.
  Context (VC : category)
          (TV : Terminal VC)
          (VP : BinProducts VC)
          (IV : Initial VC)
          (VCP : BinCoproducts VC)
          (expV : Exponentials VP)
          (V : sym_mon_closed_cat := sym_mon_closed_cartesian_cat VC VP TV expV)
          (r : V).

  Opaque V.

  (**
   1.1. The functors
   *)

VC: category
TV: Terminal VC
VP: BinProducts VC
IV: Initial VC
VCP: BinCoproducts VC
expV: Exponentials VP
V:= sym_mon_closed_cartesian_cat VC VP TV expV: sym_mon_closed_cat
r: V
∏ x y z : V,
internal_comp x y z
· internal_lam
    (sym_mon_braiding V (x ⊸ z) (z ⊸ r)
     · internal_comp x z r) =
internal_lam
  (sym_mon_braiding V (y ⊸ z) (z ⊸ r)
   · internal_comp y z r)
#⊗ internal_lam
     (sym_mon_braiding V (x ⊸ y) (y ⊸ r)
      · internal_comp x y r)
· (sym_mon_braiding V ((z ⊸ r) ⊸ y ⊸ r)
     ((y ⊸ r) ⊸ x ⊸ r)
   · internal_comp (z ⊸ r) (y ⊸ r) (x ⊸ r))

   · internal_lam

· internal_eval x r

r, x, a: V
h: V ⟦ a, x ⊸ r ⟧
a': V
h': V ⟦ a', x ⟧
(internal_id x #⊗ h) #⊗ h'
· (sym_mon_braiding V (x ⊸ x) (x ⊸ r) #⊗ identity x
   · (internal_lam
        (mon_lassociator (x ⊸ r) (x ⊸ x) x
         · (identity (x ⊸ r) #⊗ internal_eval x x
            · internal_eval x r)) #⊗ identity x
      · internal_eval x r)) =
mon_lunitor a #⊗ h'
· (h #⊗ identity x · internal_eval x r)

r: V
∏ x y z : V,
internal_comp x y z
· internal_lam
    (sym_mon_braiding V (x ⊸ z) (z ⊸ r)
     · internal_comp x z r) =
internal_lam
  (sym_mon_braiding V (y ⊸ z) (z ⊸ r)
   · internal_comp y z r)
#⊗ internal_lam
     (sym_mon_braiding V (x ⊸ y) (y ⊸ r)
      · internal_comp x y r)
· (sym_mon_braiding V ((z ⊸ r) ⊸ y ⊸ r)
     ((y ⊸ r) ⊸ x ⊸ r)
   · internal_comp (z ⊸ r) (y ⊸ r) (x ⊸ r))

r, x, y, z, a: V
h: V ⟦ a, z ⊸ r ⟧
internal_comp x y z #⊗ h
· (sym_mon_braiding V (x ⊸ z) (z ⊸ r)
   · internal_comp x z r) =
(internal_lam
   (sym_mon_braiding V (y ⊸ z) (z ⊸ r)
    · internal_comp y z r)
 #⊗ internal_lam
      (sym_mon_braiding V (x ⊸ y) (y ⊸ r)
       · internal_comp x y r)) #⊗ h
· (sym_mon_braiding V ((z ⊸ r) ⊸ y ⊸ r)
     ((y ⊸ r) ⊸ x ⊸ r) #⊗ identity (z ⊸ r)
   · (internal_comp (z ⊸ r) (y ⊸ r) (x ⊸ r)
      #⊗ identity (z ⊸ r)
      · internal_eval (z ⊸ r) (x ⊸ r)))

    · internal_comp y z r)

   · (sym_mon_braiding V (x ⊸ y) ((y ⊸ z) ⊗ (z ⊸ r))

   · internal_comp x z r)

r, x, y, z, a: V
h: V ⟦ a, x ⟧
sym_mon_braiding V ((y ⊸ z) ⊗ (x ⊸ y)) (z ⊸ r) #⊗ h
· (identity (z ⊸ r) #⊗ internal_comp x y z)
  #⊗ identity x · internal_comp x z r #⊗ identity x
· internal_eval x r =
(sym_mon_braiding V (y ⊸ z) (x ⊸ y)
 #⊗ identity (z ⊸ r)) #⊗ h
· mon_lassociator (x ⊸ y) (y ⊸ z) (z ⊸ r)
  #⊗ identity x

  #⊗ identity x
· ((sym_mon_braiding V (y ⊸ z) (z ⊸ r)
    #⊗ identity (x ⊸ y)) #⊗ identity x
   · (internal_comp y z r #⊗ identity (x ⊸ y))
     #⊗ identity x)
· internal_comp x y r #⊗ identity x
· internal_eval x r

r, x, y, z, a: V
h: V ⟦ a, x ⟧
(sym_mon_braiding V (y ⊸ z) (x ⊸ y)
 #⊗ identity (z ⊸ r)) #⊗ h
· (mon_lassociator (x ⊸ y) (y ⊸ z) (z ⊸ r)
   #⊗ identity x
   · (sym_mon_braiding V (x ⊸ y) ((y ⊸ z) ⊗ (z ⊸ r))
      #⊗ identity x
      · ((sym_mon_braiding V (y ⊸ z) (z ⊸ r)
          #⊗ identity (x ⊸ y)) #⊗ identity x
         · (mon_lassociator ((z ⊸ r) ⊗ (y ⊸ z))
              (x ⊸ y) x
            · (identity ((z ⊸ r) ⊗ (y ⊸ z))
               #⊗ internal_eval x y
               · mon_lassociator (z ⊸ r) (y ⊸ z) y))))) =
sym_mon_braiding V ((y ⊸ z) ⊗ (x ⊸ y)) (z ⊸ r) #⊗ h
· (mon_lassociator (z ⊸ r) ((y ⊸ z) ⊗ (x ⊸ y)) x
   · (identity (z ⊸ r)
      #⊗ mon_lassociator (y ⊸ z) (x ⊸ y) x
      · identity (z ⊸ r)
        #⊗ (identity (y ⊸ z) #⊗ internal_eval x y)))

VC: category
TV: Terminal VC
VP: BinProducts VC
IV: Initial VC
VCP: BinCoproducts VC
expV: Exponentials VP
V:= sym_mon_closed_cartesian_cat VC VP TV expV: sym_mon_closed_cat
r, x, y, z: V
sym_mon_braiding V (y ⊸ z) (x ⊸ y) #⊗ identity (z ⊸ r)
· mon_lassociator (x ⊸ y) (y ⊸ z) (z ⊸ r)
· sym_mon_braiding V (x ⊸ y) ((y ⊸ z) ⊗ (z ⊸ r))
· sym_mon_braiding V (y ⊸ z) (z ⊸ r)
  #⊗ identity (x ⊸ y)
· mon_lassociator (z ⊸ r) (y ⊸ z) (x ⊸ y) = ?b

VC: category
TV: Terminal VC
VP: BinProducts VC
IV: Initial VC
VCP: BinCoproducts VC
expV: Exponentials VP
V:= sym_mon_closed_cartesian_cat VC VP TV expV: sym_mon_closed_cat
r, x, y, z: V
mon_lassociator (y ⊸ z) (x ⊸ y) (z ⊸ r)
· sym_mon_braiding V (y ⊸ z) ((x ⊸ y) ⊗ (z ⊸ r))
· mon_lassociator (x ⊸ y) (z ⊸ r) (y ⊸ z)
· sym_mon_braiding V (x ⊸ y) ((z ⊸ r) ⊗ (y ⊸ z))
· mon_lassociator (z ⊸ r) (y ⊸ z) (x ⊸ y) =
sym_mon_braiding V ((y ⊸ z) ⊗ (x ⊸ y)) (z ⊸ r)

      apply lassociator_hexagon_two.
    
VC: category
TV: Terminal VC
VP: BinProducts VC
IV: Initial VC
VCP: BinCoproducts VC
expV: Exponentials VP
V:= sym_mon_closed_cartesian_cat VC VP TV expV: sym_mon_closed_cat
r: V
∏ (x y : V) (f : V ⟦ x, y ⟧),
internal_from_arr (internal_precomp f r) =
internal_from_arr f
· internal_lam
    (sym_mon_braiding V (x ⊸ y) (y ⊸ r)
     · internal_comp x y r)

VC: category
TV: Terminal VC
VP: BinProducts VC
IV: Initial VC
VCP: BinCoproducts VC
expV: Exponentials VP
V:= sym_mon_closed_cartesian_cat VC VP TV expV: sym_mon_closed_cat
r, x, y: V
f: V ⟦ x, y ⟧
∏ (a : V) (h : V ⟦ a, y ⊸ r ⟧),
internal_from_arr (internal_precomp f r) #⊗ h
· internal_eval (y ⊸ r) (x ⊸ r) =
(internal_from_arr f
 · internal_lam
     (sym_mon_braiding V (x ⊸ y) (y ⊸ r)
      · internal_comp x y r)) #⊗ h
· internal_eval (y ⊸ r) (x ⊸ r)

   · internal_comp x y r #⊗ identity x)

VC: category
TV: Terminal VC
VP: BinProducts VC
IV: Initial VC
VCP: BinCoproducts VC
expV: Exponentials VP
V:= sym_mon_closed_cartesian_cat VC VP TV expV: sym_mon_closed_cat
r, x, y: V
f: V ⟦ x, y ⟧
a: V
h: V ⟦ a, y ⊸ r ⟧
a': V
h': V ⟦ a', x ⟧
(identity I_{ V} #⊗ h) #⊗ h'
· (mon_lunitor (y ⊸ r) #⊗ identity x
   · (internal_lam
        (identity (y ⊸ r) #⊗ f · internal_eval y r)
      #⊗ identity x · internal_eval x r)) =
(internal_lam (mon_lunitor x · f) #⊗ h) #⊗ h'
· (sym_mon_braiding V (x ⊸ y) (y ⊸ r) #⊗ identity x
   · (internal_lam
        (mon_lassociator (y ⊸ r) (x ⊸ y) x
         · identity (y ⊸ r) #⊗ internal_eval x y
         · internal_eval y r) #⊗ identity x
      · internal_eval x r))

a: V
h: V ⟦ a, y ⊸ r ⟧
a': V
h': V ⟦ a', x ⟧
(identity I_{ V} #⊗ h) #⊗ h'
· (mon_lunitor (y ⊸ r) #⊗ identity x
   · (identity (y ⊸ r) #⊗ f · internal_eval y r)) =

   · (mon_lassociator (y ⊸ r) (x ⊸ y) x
      · identity (y ⊸ r) #⊗ internal_eval x y
      · internal_eval y r))

a: V
h: V ⟦ a, y ⊸ r ⟧

h': V ⟦ a', x ⟧

   · (identity (y ⊸ r) #⊗ f · internal_eval y r))

· identity (y ⊸ r) #⊗ f · internal_eval y r

VC: category

VC: category
TV: Terminal VC
VP: BinProducts VC
IV: Initial VC
VCP: BinCoproducts VC
expV: Exponentials VP
V:= sym_mon_closed_cartesian_cat VC VP TV expV: sym_mon_closed_cat
r, x, y: V
f: V ⟦ x, y ⟧
a: V
h: V ⟦ a, y ⊸ r ⟧
a': V
h': V ⟦ a', x ⟧
(internal_lam (mon_lunitor x · f) #⊗ h
 · sym_mon_braiding V (x ⊸ y) (y ⊸ r))
#⊗ (h' · identity x)
· mon_lassociator (y ⊸ r) (x ⊸ y) x
· identity (y ⊸ r) #⊗ internal_eval x y
· internal_eval y r = ?b

        
VC: category
TV: Terminal VC
VP: BinProducts VC
IV: Initial VC
VCP: BinCoproducts VC
expV: Exponentials VP
V:= sym_mon_closed_cartesian_cat VC VP TV expV: sym_mon_closed_cat
r, x, y: V
f: V ⟦ x, y ⟧
a: V
h: V ⟦ a, y ⊸ r ⟧
a': V
h': V ⟦ a', x ⟧
(sym_mon_braiding V I_{ V} a
 · h #⊗ internal_lam (mon_lunitor x · f))
#⊗ (h' · identity x)
· mon_lassociator (y ⊸ r) (x ⊸ y) x
· identity (y ⊸ r) #⊗ internal_eval x y
· internal_eval y r = ?b

  #⊗ identity x · mon_lassociator (y ⊸ r) (x ⊸ y) x

  (**
   1.2. The unit and counit
   *)
  Definition continuation_adjunction_unit_data
    : nat_trans_data
        (functor_identity V)
        (continuation_functor ∙ continuation_functor_op)
    := λ x, internal_lam (sym_mon_braiding _ _ _ · internal_eval _ _).

r, x, y: V
f: V ⟦ x, y ⟧
f
· internal_lam
    (sym_mon_braiding V (functor_identity V y)
       (functor_identity V y ⊸ r)
     · internal_eval (functor_identity V y) r) =

  (sym_mon_braiding V (functor_identity V x)
     (functor_identity V x ⊸ r)
   · internal_eval (functor_identity V x) r)

(f
 · internal_lam
     (sym_mon_braiding V (functor_identity V y)
        (functor_identity V y ⊸ r)
      · internal_eval (functor_identity V y) r)) #⊗ h
· internal_eval (y ⊸ r) r =
(internal_lam
   (sym_mon_braiding V (functor_identity V x)
      (functor_identity V x ⊸ r)
    · internal_eval (functor_identity V x) r)
 · internal_precomp (internal_precomp f r) r) #⊗ h
· internal_eval (y ⊸ r) r

  continuation_functor_enrichment
  continuation_functor_op_enrichment x y
· precomp_arr (self_enrichment V)
    ((continuation_functor ∙ continuation_functor_op)

VC: category
TV: Terminal VC
VP: BinProducts VC
IV: Initial VC
VCP: BinCoproducts VC
expV: Exponentials VP
V:= sym_mon_closed_cartesian_cat VC VP TV expV: sym_mon_closed_cat
r, x, y: V
internal_lam
  (sym_mon_braiding V (x ⊸ y) (y ⊸ r)
   · internal_comp x y r)
· internal_lam
    (sym_mon_braiding V ((y ⊸ r) ⊸ x ⊸ r)
       ((x ⊸ r) ⊸ r) · internal_comp (y ⊸ r) (x ⊸ r) r)
· precomp_arr (self_enrichment V) ((y ⊸ r) ⊸ r)
    (continuation_adjunction_unit_data x) =
identity (x ⊸ y)
· postcomp_arr (self_enrichment V) x
    (continuation_adjunction_unit_data y)

   · internal_comp x y r)
· internal_lam
    (sym_mon_braiding V ((y ⊸ r) ⊸ x ⊸ r)
       ((x ⊸ r) ⊸ r) · internal_comp (y ⊸ r) (x ⊸ r) r)
· precomp_arr (self_enrichment V) ((y ⊸ r) ⊸ r)
    (internal_lam
       (sym_mon_braiding V (functor_identity V x)
          (functor_identity V x ⊸ r)
        · internal_eval (functor_identity V x) r)) =
identity (x ⊸ y)
· postcomp_arr (self_enrichment V) x
    (internal_lam
       (sym_mon_braiding V (functor_identity V y)
          (functor_identity V y ⊸ r)
        · internal_eval (functor_identity V y) r))

V:= sym_mon_closed_cartesian_cat VC VP TV expV: sym_mon_closed_cat
r, x, y, a: V
h: V ⟦ a, x ⟧
internal_lam
  (sym_mon_braiding V (x ⊸ y) (y ⊸ r)
   · internal_comp x y r) #⊗ identity x
· (internal_lam
     (sym_mon_braiding V ((y ⊸ r) ⊸ x ⊸ r)
        ((x ⊸ r) ⊸ r)
      · internal_comp (y ⊸ r) (x ⊸ r) r) #⊗ identity x
   · (identity (((x ⊸ r) ⊸ r) ⊸ (y ⊸ r) ⊸ r)
      #⊗ internal_lam
           (sym_mon_braiding V (functor_identity V x)
              (functor_identity V x ⊸ r)
            · internal_eval (functor_identity V x) r)
      · internal_eval ((x ⊸ r) ⊸ r) ((y ⊸ r) ⊸ r))) =
internal_eval x y
· internal_lam
    (sym_mon_braiding V (functor_identity V y)
       (functor_identity V y ⊸ r)
     · internal_eval (functor_identity V y) r)

VCP: BinCoproducts VC
expV: Exponentials VP
V:= sym_mon_closed_cartesian_cat VC VP TV expV: sym_mon_closed_cat
r, x, y, a: V
h: V ⟦ a, x ⟧
a': V
h': V ⟦ a', y ⊸ r ⟧
mon_lassociator x ((y ⊸ r) ⊸ x ⊸ r) (y ⊸ r)
· internal_lam
    (sym_mon_braiding V (functor_identity V x)
       (functor_identity V x ⊸ r)
     · internal_eval (functor_identity V x) r)
  #⊗ (identity ((y ⊸ r) ⊸ x ⊸ r) #⊗ identity (y ⊸ r))
· identity ((x ⊸ r) ⊸ r)
  #⊗ internal_eval (y ⊸ r) (x ⊸ r)
· internal_eval (x ⊸ r) r = ?t2

VC: category
TV: Terminal VC
VP: BinProducts VC
IV: Initial VC
VCP: BinCoproducts VC
expV: Exponentials VP
V:= sym_mon_closed_cartesian_cat VC VP TV expV: sym_mon_closed_cat
r, x, y, a: V
h: V ⟦ a, x ⟧
a': V
h': V ⟦ a', y ⊸ r ⟧
(internal_lam
   (sym_mon_braiding V (x ⊸ y) (y ⊸ r)
    · internal_comp x y r) #⊗ identity x) #⊗ h'
· (sym_mon_braiding V ((y ⊸ r) ⊸ x ⊸ r) x
   #⊗ identity (y ⊸ r)
   · (mon_lassociator x ((y ⊸ r) ⊸ x ⊸ r) (y ⊸ r)
      · (internal_lam
           (sym_mon_braiding V (functor_identity V x)
              (functor_identity V x ⊸ r)
            · internal_eval (functor_identity V x) r)
         #⊗ (identity ((y ⊸ r) ⊸ x ⊸ r)
             #⊗ identity (y ⊸ r))
         · (identity ((x ⊸ r) ⊸ r)
            #⊗ internal_eval (y ⊸ r) (x ⊸ r)
            · internal_eval (x ⊸ r) r)))) =
internal_eval x y #⊗ h'
· (sym_mon_braiding V (functor_identity V y)
     (functor_identity V y ⊸ r)
   · internal_eval (functor_identity V y) r)

        (functor_identity V x ⊸ r)
      · internal_eval (functor_identity V x) r)
   #⊗ identity (x ⊸ r) · internal_eval (x ⊸ r) r) =
?t2

  (sym_mon_braiding V (functor_identity V y)
     (functor_identity V y ⊸ r)
   · internal_eval (functor_identity V y) r)

    (sym_mon_braiding V (functor_identity V x)

VC: category
TV: Terminal VC
VP: BinProducts VC
IV: Initial VC
VCP: BinCoproducts VC
expV: Exponentials VP
V:= sym_mon_closed_cartesian_cat VC VP TV expV: sym_mon_closed_cat
r: V
x, y: V ^opp
p:= nat_trans_enrichment_to_comp
  continuation_adjunction_unit_enrichment y x: internal_lam
  (sym_mon_braiding V (y ⊸ x) (x ⊸ r)
   · internal_comp y x r)
· internal_lam
    (sym_mon_braiding V ((x ⊸ r) ⊸ y ⊸ r)
       ((y ⊸ r) ⊸ r)
     · internal_comp (x ⊸ r) (y ⊸ r) r)
· precomp_arr (self_enrichment V) 
    ((x ⊸ r) ⊸ r)
    (continuation_adjunction_unit_data y) =
identity (y ⊸ x)
· postcomp_arr (self_enrichment V) y
    (continuation_adjunction_unit_data x)
identity (y ⊸ x)
· precomp_arr (op_enrichment V (self_enrichment V)) y
    (continuation_adjunction_unit_data x) =
internal_lam
  (sym_mon_braiding V (y ⊸ x) (x ⊸ r)
   · internal_comp y x r)
· internal_lam
    (sym_mon_braiding V ((x ⊸ r) ⊸ y ⊸ r)
       ((y ⊸ r) ⊸ r) · internal_comp (x ⊸ r) (y ⊸ r) r)
· postcomp_arr (op_enrichment V (self_enrichment V))
    ((x ⊸ r) ⊸ r)
    (continuation_adjunction_unit_data y)

  continuation_adjunction_unit_enrichment y x: internal_lam
  (sym_mon_braiding V (y ⊸ x) (x ⊸ r)
   · internal_comp y x r)

r, x, a: V
h: V ⟦ a, x ⟧
identity (x ⊸ r)
#⊗ (h
    · internal_lam
        (sym_mon_braiding V (functor_identity V x)
           (functor_identity V x ⊸ r)
         · internal_eval (functor_identity V x) r))
· (sym_mon_braiding V (functor_identity V (x ⊸ r))
     (functor_identity V (x ⊸ r) ⊸ r)
   · internal_eval (functor_identity V (x ⊸ r)) r) =
identity (x ⊸ r) #⊗ h · internal_eval x r

r, x, a: V

identity (x ⊸ r)
#⊗ (h
    · internal_lam
        (sym_mon_braiding V (functor_identity V x)

         · internal_eval (functor_identity V x) r))
· sym_mon_braiding V (functor_identity V (x ⊸ r))
    (functor_identity V (x ⊸ r) ⊸ r)
· internal_eval (functor_identity V (x ⊸ r)) r =

  Defined.

  Definition continuation_enriched_adjunction
    : enriched_adjunction
        (self_enrichment V)
        (op_enrichment V (self_enrichment V))
    := continuation_adjunction ,, continuation_adjunction_enrichment.
End ContinuationAdjunction.

(**
 2. The continuation model
 *)
Section ContinuationModel.
  Context (VC : category)
          (TV : Terminal VC)
          (VP : BinProducts VC)
          (IV : Initial VC)
          (VCP : BinCoproducts VC)
          (expV : Exponentials VP)
          (V : sym_mon_closed_cat := sym_mon_closed_cartesian_cat VC VP TV expV)
          (r : V).

  Definition continuation_eec_model
    : eec_model
    := VC
       ,,
       TV
       ,,
       VP
       ,,
       expV
       ,,
       (VC^opp)
       ,,
       op_enrichment _ (self_enrichment V)
       ,,
       continuation_enriched_adjunction V TV VP expV r
       ,,
       opposite_terminal_enriched _ (self_enrichment_initial V IV)
       ,,
       opposite_initial_enriched _ (self_enrichment_terminal V TV)
       ,,
       opposite_enrichment_power _ (self_enrichment_copowers V)
       ,,
       opposite_enrichment_copower _ (self_enrichment_powers V)
       ,,
       (opposite_enrichment_binary_prod
          (self_enrichment V)
          (self_enrichment_binary_coproducts V VCP))
       ,,
       (opposite_enrichment_binary_coprod
          (self_enrichment V)
          (self_enrichment_binary_products V VP)).

  Definition continuation_eec_plus_model
    : eec_plus_model
    := continuation_eec_model ,, IV ,, VCP.
End ContinuationModel.
